<rate>5</rate>< Review>
Love this place.. They are open 24/7 to print, copy, work, etc... also desktop pc's for customers to use around the clock.. They also have work stations with scissors, cutting boards, glue, rulers, white out, pens, staplers, and paper clips available for your project at no extra cost.  The employees are friendly and helpful when asked.  They have great clearance items around the store.  The store is organized and clean, the restrooms are also clean.  They have everything needed for shipping... this is a great place for night owls like myself...

Add on:
Thanks Orlando and Sean for your help shipping a very large package tonight.. Again FedEx has great helpful Employees and I needed help with this package.</Review>

< Review>
As far as martial arts go, you really cant beat Brazilian Jiu-Jitsu and as far as training with some of the best practitioners of BJJ, you cant beat Professors AnaLaura and Rafael. They are an inspiring couple who came to this country with little financial means, but pursued a dream to be the best in the world in their field. Professor Ana is a multiple-time world champion and her proficiency on the mat is matched by her dedication to the students. Not only are they champions on the mat, but in their mentality and approach to life. Every parent should want their kids to have mentors that help incubate the confidence and strength of character that is desperately needed in today's culture.

GB Upland is a family friendly environment where kids develop life-skills on the mat that will sustain them throughout life, but the Academy also offers high-level competition training where students from all over are looking to test their skills on the competition circuit.

Whether you are wanting to shed some extra pounds, develop confidence and self-discipline, train with world champions, or just love rolling on the mat and practicing the art, you will not be disappointed at GB Upland.< /Review>

We were referred to Dr. Yazdi by our lactation consultant, Paula Santi, as a result of chronic breastfeeding issues (pain and recurring clogged ducts due to baby‚Äôs inefficient eating). Our LC recommended that we have a consultation for tight frenulum and consider frenectomy. We sought consultations with 2 doctors from Kaiser because we initially wanted to stay within our insurance network if we did decide to have the procedure. However, both Kaiser doctors seemed to know little about the mechanics of breastfeeding and convinced us that it was unlikely the procedure would have any effect on our breastfeeding experience. After the Kaiser consultations, we didn‚Äôt think we would have the procedure done. However, we didn‚Äôt want to give up hope of being able to breastfeed our son. So, when we shared the Kaiser experience with Paula, she suggested that we see Dr. Yazdi. I can‚Äôt even begin to say how happy I am that we took her advice. Dr. Yazdi was very knowledgeable on the subject as well as how ties impact the mechanics of breastfeeding. He took his time answer our extensive questions, and really listened to our concerns. We did not feel pressured at all to have the procedure. In response to others who say that he comes on strong, like he‚Äôs making a sales pitch, I would say, in our experience, he does have a ‚Äúpitch‚Äù but I think that he‚Äôs just trying to explain the mechanics of breastfeeding and how the anatomy of the baby‚Äôs mouth needs to work together to breastfeed effectively. This involves educating the patient, and my husband and I appreciated that educational piece of the consultation; perhaps others do not. Also, I‚Äôm not questioning others who say he pressured them to have the procedure...maybe he did. But, that was not our experience. He gave us the room to talk it over, and we decided to have the tongue and lip tie corrected that day. The procedure itself was incredibly fast. The baby came out with a little blood on his lip. We were told that is normal, and, indeed, the bleeding stopped right away, and he nursed immediately. The first feed I used a nipple shield so could not gauge if the pain associated with his latch diminished, but he seemed to be eating pretty efficiently. The second feed after the procedure I nursed without the use of the shield and that‚Äôs when I became a firm believer that this procedure can have amazing results. After months of struggling with blistered and bleeding nipples, my baby finally latched with no pain and had a full feed in 30 minutes. He was so milk drunk afterwards. It was amazing. He did become pretty fussy that night and we were assured that‚Äôs to be expected. Since the procedure yesterday we‚Äôve had multiple feeds without the use of the nipple shield, with no pain to me and a well fed, satisfied baby. I know that this doesn‚Äôt work for everyone and that results are not always so immediate, but for us it was incredible, and I‚Äôm so glad we decided to have it done by Dr. Yazdi and his wonderful team!<//text>

< text>
I love that there are several sandwich options in this neighborhood. I was intrigued by the italian sandwiches from Handy Deli and decided to try it out a couple of weeks ago.

I got the Bella Vista, which has a mountain of prosciutto, fresh mozz, and grilled eggplant, with a walnut pesto spread and finished on a panini press. Every italian sandwich comes with a side salad, which is great! All in all, it was delicious, but it was just a tiiiiiiny bit too salty. Next time, will have to try a different sandwich. I'm particularly interested in the bistro sandwich.

The deli is quite small and gets a bit crowded around lunch time. I suggest calling ahead so you don't have to wait inside for your order< /text>

< Review>
Awesome little nondescript deli on the corner of 19th and Irving. Stopped in for a snack on the way to the airport. Straight forward liquor store with fifteen foot wall ceilings of just about every bottle you can imagine, plus a big wine selection (cold also available). But tucked into a corner near the cash register is a selection of grab-and-go homemade items like hummus, falafel, and dolmas. Such good quality food!! Will absolutely make this a stop every time I head to SFO.<//Review>

< Name>
Eric Tam<//Name>
<date>1612287810757<//date><rating>5</rating>< Text>
One of my new favorite local go to places. You get lot of food for your money. They pack and pack and pack until the lid barely closes.

Start with either their Fried Pork Won-Ton or Salt and Pepper Chicken Wings. Go with their Chicken or BBQ Pork Fried Rice and ChiceknChow Mein. For white rice, you can't go wrong with their version of savory Peking Pork Chops and mild Curry Chicken (ask them for extra sauce). The Curry Chicken is not like the Indian type curry that's loaded with spices, and it is not like the Thai curry but it's somewhere in between.  Round it off with some simple fresh vegetables (you can ask them what is fresh) with garlic sauce.

For those that are more adventurous, try their Running Egg and Shrimp over Chow Fun.  It's an egg-gravy style over Chow Fun that's designed to be eaten right away but if you are an egg-lover, this is a must try. Or, opt for their version of Crispy Fried Noodle where the Crispy Noodles come in a box and you get a container of the sauce and toppings to pour on top when you are ready to eat. Another thing to try is their "Eight Treasure Tofu Special" with some white rice, or if it's in season, go for the comfort type food "Bitter Melon and Beef".

And, make sure you order a side of their mini sesame balls that is a great as a palate cleanser, or to go with a cup of tea.

Staff here are very friendly and all their regulars greet the staff here by name, and vice versa. Through it all, they kept things frugal with their decor and limit to what's necessary for good quality food to keep prices low for their customers.</Text>

< Review>
My very first order from Yelp24!  This meal was enough to feed an army.  I will be eating left overs for days.

I ordered Kung Pao chicken, pan fried noodle special and pork fried rice.  I received egg rolls for free courtesy of Yelp24.

I immediately ate all the crispy (not soggy) rolls.  They tasted like a little piece of heaven or something like that!  Kung Pao chicken was also excellent.  I forgot to recommend spicy when I placed the order but still very tasty.  I was so full but I managed to try the pan fried noodles and I thought it was excellent. Reminded me Top Roman but much better.  It had bok Choy, fish, carrots and some tasty spices.  I wish I would of asked for spicy!

The order came quickly. Fifteen minutes earlier!  That was a first!  I was shocked!

Great meal and lots of left overs!< /Review>

<user_id>114479080778506572357<//user_id><user_name>Ron Wenger<//user_name>< Time>
1474402390524</Time>
<Rating>4< /Rating>< Text>
I played the course for the first time while visiting family on Friday September 16.  The course was in overall good shape.  Some of the greens are very big with nice curves.  Noted the lip of the cups were not groomed which caused several missed putts. You have to hit almost dead center to sink a putt.  Also noted numerous ball marks and debris on the greens that needed repair to no fault of the course greens keeper.  (Fix your ball marks guys and gals!!)    Front nine featured some very narrow fairways which proved unfriendly to a fade or draw.  The back nine opened up some and the water holes provided a fair challenge.  Overall I would play the course again when in the area.  A suggestion would be to provide a map of the course, of some signage, that would assist a person, not from the area, with finding the holes on the back nine.  Had to use a number of paved streets to navigate and if I were not with a local, I would still be lost.<//Text>
